--- layout: default title: "BigBinTxt - TXT Record with Multiple Binary Strings" parent: "Fuzzing" --- BigBinTxt - TXT Record with Multiple Binary Strings

BigBinTxt - TXT Record with Multiple Binary Strings

This module is designed to respond with a single TXT record containing any number of labels, each with an arbitrary size.

This flexibility allows for generating very large DNS responses, up to the maximum allowable DNS packet size of 65535 bytes.

In this variant, the labels are composed of random binary data.

Category: Fuzzing

RFCs: RFC1035, RFC1464

Format

bigbintxt.<LABELS>.<SIZE>.yourdomain.com

Where:

  • The <LABELS> parameter specifies the number of labels to be included in the TXT record.

  • The <SIZE> parameter specifies the number of bytes in each label. Note that the maximum possible size for a TXT label is 255 bytes as per DNS implementation.

Examples

In this example, we request to produce a TXT record containing a single label consisting of 50 random bytes:

# dig bigbintxt.1.50.yourdomain.com @127.0.0.1

; <<>> DiG 9.18.10-2-Debian <<>> bigbintxt.1.50.yourdomain.com @127.0.0.1
;; global options: +cmd
;; Got answer:
;; ->>HEADER<<- opcode: QUERY, status: NOERROR, id: 15882
;; flags: qr aa; QUERY: 1, ANSWER: 1, AUTHORITY: 0, ADDITIONAL: 0

;; QUESTION SECTION:
;bigbintxt.1.50.yourdomain.com.	IN	A

;; ANSWER SECTION:
bigbintxt.1.50.yourdomain.com. 60 IN	TXT	"\205\127\140\141\175\230w\1442\249\001\255\221\141!\170&\233\227\019\142\238\207\195X\157\020J5>\008\012[\212\132\176o*A\150h\245\031\181\233\139\188\194#\186"

;; Query time: 3 msec
;; SERVER: 127.0.0.1#53(127.0.0.1) (UDP)
;; WHEN: Fri Jan 03 09:42:56 +04 2025
;; MSG SIZE  rcvd: 110

Download PCAP File


In this example, we request to produce a TXT record containing a single label consisting of 255 random bytes, which is the maximum allowable size for a TXT label:

# dig bigbintxt.1.255.yourdomain.com @127.0.0.1

; <<>> DiG 9.18.10-2-Debian <<>> bigbintxt.1.255.yourdomain.com @127.0.0.1
;; global options: +cmd
;; Got answer:
;; ->>HEADER<<- opcode: QUERY, status: NOERROR, id: 7423
;; flags: qr aa; QUERY: 1, ANSWER: 1, AUTHORITY: 0, ADDITIONAL: 0

;; QUESTION SECTION:
;bigbintxt.1.255.yourdomain.com.	IN	A

;; ANSWER SECTION:
bigbintxt.1.255.yourdomain.com.	60 IN	TXT	"\219o\219g\152O\030\188\240*j\164\163Q\148\210\199\131\185\174%tR\229\1966\240H\140\155}\189\012#\205\024\021\160\026\211\027\233/\129\129>\224\018\028\190h\204\031H\140\192\159\143\189\1402C\174FI\251\165\187\013eRz\194\253\152\205\238#\167\137R\231\031\211\152K\163\234\219\149\185\2120 \192\028\180\142\192+pA\027\004\023V\195\252\248Z\254\198\156\014K\006\170\243\"\198Z|\138\163\0149j\192\144\163|\029f\188\147'\197\251\005\171\255D\244\227\165\254\244\208k\229dd\198R\188c\241\141\220\205\190:\127\161}\209~\008\191\\r\170S\220\015?rVOj\025 c+\161\214gh\150\185\031B):\140\026B\029i-\231!MV\183\154\009\134^!\010\140\192\232\158T\187I\129\254=\244\214\175eV\1276\010s\220\000\141\159\167V\147Rx\196\191}2\223Y\211\002`=\178\000\003\199\011\197"

;; Query time: 0 msec
;; SERVER: 127.0.0.1#53(127.0.0.1) (UDP)
;; WHEN: Fri Jan 03 09:42:57 +04 2025
;; MSG SIZE  rcvd: 316

Download PCAP File


In this example, we request to produce a TXT record with 255 labels, each containing a single random byte:

# dig bigbintxt.255.1.yourdomain.com @127.0.0.1

; <<>> DiG 9.18.10-2-Debian <<>> bigbintxt.255.1.yourdomain.com @127.0.0.1
;; global options: +cmd
;; Got answer:
;; ->>HEADER<<- opcode: QUERY, status: NOERROR, id: 51862
;; flags: qr aa; QUERY: 1, ANSWER: 1, AUTHORITY: 0, ADDITIONAL: 0

;; QUESTION SECTION:
;bigbintxt.255.1.yourdomain.com.	IN	A

;; ANSWER SECTION:

;; Query time: 0 msec
;; SERVER: 127.0.0.1#53(127.0.0.1) (UDP)
;; WHEN: Fri Jan 03 09:42:58 +04 2025
;; MSG SIZE  rcvd: 570

Download PCAP File

Note that there is no limit on the number of labels. The only restriction is the maximum DNS packet size of 65535 bytes.


In this example, we request to produce a TXT record with 10000 labels, each containing a single random byte:

# dig bigbintxt.10000.1.yourdomain.com @127.0.0.1

; <<>> DiG 9.18.10-2-Debian <<>> bigbintxt.10000.1.yourdomain.com @127.0.0.1
;; global options: +cmd
;; Got answer:
;; ->>HEADER<<- opcode: QUERY, status: NOERROR, id: 7831
;; flags: qr aa; QUERY: 1, ANSWER: 1, AUTHORITY: 0, ADDITIONAL: 0

;bigbintxt.10000.1.yourdomain.com. IN	A

;; ANSWER SECTION:
